# Benchmark: [POSTGRES DISK] pgbench TPC-B - PostgreSQL OLTP

**Date:** 2026-01-04 08:17:10
**Scenario:** PostgreSQL OLTP - 100 clients, TPC-B like workload with full monitoring

## Command 1: Begin:sysctl_swappiness

### Command
```bash
sysctl -w vm.swappiness=1
```

### Output
```

```

## Command 7: pgbench

### Command
```bash
sudo -u postgres pgbench -c 100 -j 32 -T 60 -P 5 -b tpcb-like pgbench
```

### Output

---

## Command 11: pg_wait_events

### Command
```bash
bash -c 'for i in $(seq 1 70); do echo "=== $(date '"'"'+%H:%M:%S'"'"') ==="; sudo -u postgres psql -t -c "SELECT coalesce(wait_event_type,'"'"'CPU'"'"') as type, coalesce(wait_event,'"'"'Running'"'"') as event, count(*) as cnt FROM pg_stat_activity WHERE state='"'"'active'"'"' AND pid<>pg_backend_pid() GROUP BY 1,2 ORDER BY 3 DESC LIMIT 10"; sleep 1; done'
```
